#### Understanding why synthetic data is privacy-safe
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=0)** - It's arguably the most important characteristic of an anonymization technology to actually protect your customers' privacy.
>
> **[0:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=8)** So why is synthetic data privacy safe?
>
> **[0:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=11)** The important bit to take away here is that not all synthetic data is anonymous by default.
>
> **[0:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=17)** Not all synthetic data is able or even aimed to protect privacy.
>
> **[0:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=22)** Therefore, it's important for any synthetic data generator that wants to produce fully anonymous synthetic data to come with the necessary privacy mechanisms and privacy measures and tests that tell you whether the generator synthetic data is anonymous or not.
>
> **[0:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=37)** There isn't really one list of which privacy mechanisms need to go into a synthetic data generator, but there are a few things that you should look out for when evaluating synthetic data tools and solutions.
>
> **[0:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=49)** First, we discussed that one of the big pitfalls of legacy anonymization is that there still remains real data in the supposedly anonymous dataset, and even if it's just a little bit, that's often sufficient for re-identification.
>
> **[1:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=63)** So one advantage of synthetic data is that there's no one-to-one relationship between any synthetic data point and any real-world human being.
>
> **[1:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=73)** And to make this happen, one of the most important things that you need to implement is to prevent overfitting of your synthetic data generator.
>
> **[1:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=81)** It needs to be set up in a way that it only learns statistically generalizable patterns in your dataset, but doesn't learn the training dataset by heart or too closely, because if that happens, it might accidentally include personal secrets or privacy-sensitive information in your synthetic data, and that's not good.
>
> **[1:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=101)** So prevention of overfitting and no one-to-one relationship between your original data and the synthetic data is an important element to significantly reduce the attack surface from a privacy point of view.
>
> **[1:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=115)** A second element why synthetic data generators can produce fully anonymous synthetic data is that you have noise addition in the process.
>
> **[2:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=123)** Why?
>
> **[2:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=124)** Well, if you train a model, what you get is a probabilistic model, which then, when you generate synthetic data, randomly draws from the probability distribution, and this introduces a certain level of noise.
>
> **[2:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=137)** A third element that's highly recommended to not only protect the distribution but also the value range of your data are things like rare category protection or extreme value protection.
>
> **[2:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=148)** What is rare category protection?
>
> **[2:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=150)** Think of an organization which has information about the job titles of the customers.
>
> **[2:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=155)** If you were to find a synthetic individual whose job title is something like the Pope or the Dalai Lama, then it is highly likely that the only Pope or Dalai Lama in the world would be customers of these institutions, and this is, of course, a privacy violation.
>
> **[2:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=172)** Therefore, it's important to protect rare categories like home countries that appear seldom in the dataset, rare job professions, rare medical diagnosis, and any elements which are highly unique or only appear a handful of times in your training dataset.
>
> **[3:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=187)** They need to be excluded in the pre-processing before you synthesize them to ensure effective value range protection.
>
> **[3:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=195)** Or as another example, extreme value protection to not include the extreme numerical outliers in your synthetic training data.
>
> **[3:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=204)** So let's think of an organization having just three customers who are above 110, 115, 117, 105, whatever years old.
>
> **[3:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=213)** This appears so seldomly that it already could be a privacy infringement, and therefore, it's important to pre-process the data in a manner that extreme numerical outliers are removed.
>
> **[3:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=224)** This doesn't mean, however, that you can't learn something about the outer edges of your distribution.
>
> **[3:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=229)** Remember, most organizations synthesize datasets with millions of customers.
>
> **[3:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=234)** So if you don't get the patterns of one individual or three individuals, you still can get down very granular, and that's the advantage of synthetic data, because you can preserve so much diversity while at the same time protecting the extreme outliers that need special care whenever you anonymize data.
>
> **[4:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=252)** And finally, the most important element, regardless of which privacy mechanisms you have implemented.
>
> **[4:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=259)** One of the above, differential privacy, it doesn't matter.
>
> **[4:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=262)** You always need to empirically measure and evaluate the level of anonymity that you have achieved and to see if your mechanisms are actually working when you put them on the road.
>
> **[4:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=272)** And there are different ways to do this, but it's more of an advanced topic.
>
> **[4:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/understanding-why-synthetic-data-is-privacy-safe?u=76281980&t=276)** So if you're curious to learn more here, there are more resources provided in the Data Science handout which comes along with this course.

#### Quick recap: What is Responsible AI?
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/quick-recap-what-is-responsible-ai?u=76281980)

>
> **[0:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/quick-recap-what-is-responsible-ai?u=76281980&t=9)** Responsible AI is the practice of developing and deploying AI that puts humans first.

#### AI fairness and algorithmic bias mitigation
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980)

>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=0)** - AI has a bias problem.
>
> **[0:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=3)** It has been shown that AI discriminates against women, against people of color, against people of different sexual orientations and many many more sensitive attributes.
>
> **[0:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=13)** But it's not that the AI is inherently biased or even evil.
>
> **[0:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=17)** It's many, many different reasons why bias finds its way into the AI algorithms that we use today.
>
> **[0:23](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=23)** And data is oftentimes seen as the biggest problem of it.
>
> **[0:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=27)** Why?
>
> **[0:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=28)** You might wonder.
>
> **[0:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=29)** Well, plenty of reasons but one is insufficient training data.
>
> **[0:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=33)** AI needs plenty of examples to work from, and if you don't have enough examples for minority groups than the performance of the system suffers and doesn't function properly for minority individuals.
>
> **[0:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=45)** A second problem is that we as humans are biased and so is the data that AI is trained on.
>
> **[0:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=50)** This historic data reflects things that don't hold true anymore.
>
> **[0:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=54)** For example, if you want to use AI in hiring and make decisions about whom to invite to an interview, if you train on historic data where higher management positions were mainly occupied by male individuals, then this could significantly impact the decisions that your algorithm is going to do.
>
> **[1:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=71)** The third point is debiasing data is something that's exceptionally hard to do.
>
> **[1:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=77)** Removing sensitive attributes like gender or ethnicity is not a good option.
>
> **[1:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=82)** In fact, research has shown that you have to have these attributes in your data to make state-of-the-art fairness work in machine learning.
>
> **[1:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=90)** Interestingly, also, privacy is something that is sometimes intention with fairness.
>
> **[1:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=95)** A 2021 Microsoft survey once found amongst leading fairness practitioners that the biggest challenge they face in practice is that they don't even know whether the model biased or not.
>
> **[1:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=107)** How could it be?
>
> **[1:48](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=108)** Privacy and anti-discrimination laws.
>
> **[1:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=110)** Because they oftentimes prohibit that sensitive attributes are being used, and this leads to them operating in the blind and not being able to see if an algorithm discriminates against people of certain ethnicities or sexual orientations, for example.
>
> **[2:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=125)** Synthetic data can contribute to AI fairness in various ways, but importantly I say contribute.
>
> **[2:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=132)** It's not sufficient to only use synthetic data to overcome AI biases.
>
> **[2:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=137)** In fact, fairness is a complex topic and you need to take care of it right from the beginning when starting to develop your algorithm throughout the entire life cycle of development and deployment.
>
> **[2:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=148)** But how can synthetic data help?
>
> **[2:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=151)** The first way, how it helps is it can give you access to these important sensitive attributes in a privacy safe manner and allow teams to already see if there are some bias problems during the development and testing phase.
>
> **[2:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=165)** The second benefit of synthetic data for fairness is that it allows you to get access to data from different geographic regions particularly large organizations which are developing models that will be deployed around the globe oftentimes face challenges of not being able to get data from other regions and subsidiaries in.
>
> **[3:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=185)** Here synthetic data can allow them to get a much more geographically diverse data set that then in turn functions more equally for the different cultural groups that will be using the AI system.
>
> **[3:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=196)** And another quite interesting component is that synthetic data can be molded, rebalanced or even made fairer, for example.
>
> **[3:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=205)** You can create a data set where things like the gender pay gap are eliminated which can benefit the downstream models don't perpetuate this unwanted historic biases.
>
> **[3:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=216)** And the last point, how synthetic data can contribute to AI fairness in a major way is that it makes it possible to share data externally with fairness experts, and more importantly so with AI bias auditors, because as a human auditor it's not possible that you just look at the code of a model alone, put a stamp on it and say, well this model is not going to discriminate.
>
> **[3:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=238)** You need to have access to granular representative data that has plenty of examples in there of different individuals, minority groups and outliers to better understand if there's a bias problem or not.
>
> **[4:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/ai-fairness-and-algorithmic-bias-mitigation?u=76281980&t=251)** And this brings us to our next topic of explainable AI, where having access to data is equally important.

#### XAI
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/xai?u=76281980)

>

>
> **[0:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/xai?u=76281980&t=14)** Now, if an AI algorithm is used to decide whether you're credit worthy, should get hired, or undergo a medical procedure, and I'm not saying that AI should be used for all of this, but just as a hypothetical example, affected individuals will expect, or even demand, an explanation, and rightfully so.
>

>

>
> **[1:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/xai?u=76281980&t=89)** Because we as humans, we can't reason upon code alone, particularly not the complete decision boundaries of enormous modern-day machinery models, with their millions of model parameters.
>

>

>
> **[2:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/xai?u=76281980&t=136)** And this again is an area that can be catered to with synthetic data, where you can not only put granular privacy-safe data with plenty of diverse examples into the hands of your internal AI assurance teams, but also external auditors, certification bodies, and authorities.

> **[3:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/hands-on-synthetic-data-for-explainable-ai?u=76281980&t=210)** Some neighborhoods make it more likely that a listing will be classified as expensive while others make it more likely that the listing will cost below $100 per night.
>
> **[3:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/hands-on-synthetic-data-for-explainable-ai?u=76281980&t=221)** But just to speed through a little bit I want to show you the dependency plot of the property type.
>
> **[3:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/hands-on-synthetic-data-for-explainable-ai?u=76281980&t=226)** When looking at the dependency plot of the property type one could actually assume that this should have a very high feature importance for the overall classification.
>
> **[3:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/hands-on-synthetic-data-for-explainable-ai?u=76281980&t=235)** But if you think back to the plot we looked at earlier with the feature importance the property type was not nearly as impactful as the number of guests that a property accommodates.
>
> **[4:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/hands-on-synthetic-data-for-explainable-ai?u=76281980&t=247)** And the reason for that is because these more extreme scenarios like an Airbnb accommodation being a room in a boutique hotel don't appear in our data sample very often.
>
> **[4:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/hands-on-synthetic-data-for-explainable-ai?u=76281980&t=257)** So they're not that impactful for the overall feature importance.
>
> **[4:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/hands-on-synthetic-data-for-explainable-ai?u=76281980&t=264)** And what we can also do with SHAP values if we scroll down a little bit, is looking at the SHAP values for specific single synthetic samples to more in depth study factors behind the model scores by inspecting individual samples.
>
> **[4:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/hands-on-synthetic-data-for-explainable-ai?u=76281980&t=280)** And this is very interesting because this level of explainability simply wouldn't be possible with real data.
>
> **[4:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/hands-on-synthetic-data-for-explainable-ai?u=76281980&t=287)** It's not okay from a privacy point of view to browse through each individual customer, but you can do that with synthetic data because it's privacy safe.
>
> **[4:56](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/hands-on-synthetic-data-for-explainable-ai?u=76281980&t=296)** And therefore, synthetic data allows you to reason around samples at any scale the entire dataset or just individual samples and particularly extreme values and outliers even if they're artificially created by injecting your human expertise and understanding of our world's diversity when generating more diverse synthetic data.
>
> **[5:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/hands-on-synthetic-data-for-explainable-ai?u=76281980&t=321)** So we can, for example, look at a random sample.
>
> **[5:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/hands-on-synthetic-data-for-explainable-ai?u=76281980&t=325)** So what you can see here with the colors nicely representing it, what actually led to this record being classified as being a more expensive accomodation that costs above $100 per night.
>
> **[5:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/hands-on-synthetic-data-for-explainable-ai?u=76281980&t=338)** And a big factor was, in this case the response time that the host responded within an hour or that two nights were the minimum nights of stays that you had to have to book this recommendation.
>
> **[5:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/hands-on-synthetic-data-for-explainable-ai?u=76281980&t=350)** And then, as I mentioned earlier you can also look at the outliers and for example show the sample with the absolute lowest score.
>
> **[5:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/hands-on-synthetic-data-for-explainable-ai?u=76281980&t=358)** It's very close to zero.
>
> **[5:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/hands-on-synthetic-data-for-explainable-ai?u=76281980&t=359)** And here all the factors that contributed to the model being so confident that this property should be available for less than $100 per night, for example that it only accommodates one person and that it was a shared room in a rental unit.
>
> **[6:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/hands-on-synthetic-data-for-explainable-ai?u=76281980&t=374)** I definitely would also not have paid more than $100 for this.
>
> **[6:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/hands-on-synthetic-data-for-explainable-ai?u=76281980&t=379)** So there you have it.
>
> **[6:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/hands-on-synthetic-data-for-explainable-ai?u=76281980&t=381)** With synthetic data, you can gain a deeper understanding into why a model came to its decisions and you can do explainable AI without having to use privacy sensitive real world data.

#### Synthetic data for RAI assurance and governance
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/synthetic-data-for-rai-assurance-and-governance?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/synthetic-data-for-rai-assurance-and-governance?u=76281980&t=0)** - To understand why responsible AI assurance and AI governance are so important it's helpful to take a step back and look at the intersection of economy, society, and technology from a high level perspective.
>
> **[0:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/synthetic-data-for-rai-assurance-and-governance?u=76281980&t=14)** The objective of many nations and political and economical unions at the moment is to become a global leader in artificial intelligence in the coming years.
>
> **[0:23](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/synthetic-data-for-rai-assurance-and-governance?u=76281980&t=23)** But if we look at the status quo, currently we only have a few large organizations really using and developing artificial intelligence.
>
> **[0:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/synthetic-data-for-rai-assurance-and-governance?u=76281980&t=31)** So as a consequence, it becomes necessary that more small and medium enterprises and in general many more organizations develop and deploy artificial intelligence.
>
> **[0:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/synthetic-data-for-rai-assurance-and-governance?u=76281980&t=43)** But at the same time, already today we have this global AI talent shortage and an even bigger responsible AI talent shortage.
>
> **[0:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/synthetic-data-for-rai-assurance-and-governance?u=76281980&t=51)** Now, if we're going to have more people develop AI who have less experience with it, particularly with the ethical and responsible AI parts of it how as a government, as a regulator, can we make sure that the AI that is put out in the world actually satisfies our responsible and trustworthy AI requirements?
>
> **[1:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/synthetic-data-for-rai-assurance-and-governance?u=76281980&t=70)** And this is why responsible AI assurance and responsible AI governance ecosystems will be increasingly important.
>
> **[1:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/synthetic-data-for-rai-assurance-and-governance?u=76281980&t=77)** They should help scale the efforts of developing and using AI that adheres to regulation and societal values.
>
> **[1:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/synthetic-data-for-rai-assurance-and-governance?u=76281980&t=84)** It's really about having an ecosystem full of responsible AI tools, services, consultancy firms and even things like audits, like an audit for AI bias or certifications of algorithms that are applied for high risk use cases.
>
> **[1:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/synthetic-data-for-rai-assurance-and-governance?u=76281980&t=99)** But many of those services rely on exchanging granular data with external partners or auditors.
>
> **[1:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/synthetic-data-for-rai-assurance-and-governance?u=76281980&t=107)** And this is where synthetic data comes in as it allows to share granular data with external partners across this responsible AI assurance ecosystem.
>
> **[1:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/synthetic-data-for-rai-assurance-and-governance?u=76281980&t=117)** And this whole topic is actually something that not only regulators and societies are interested in but also organizations and for-profit businesses because for many executives, it's particularly these hard to assess more mushy risks of AI ethics and responsible AI that's currently holding them back to adopt AI more freely throughout the organization.
>
> **[2:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/synthetic-data-for-rai-assurance-and-governance?u=76281980&t=138)** Responsible AI is a highly important topic that more and more C-suites and boards are looking into particularly with all the regulation coming down the pipe like the European Union's AI Act.
>
> **[2:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/synthetic-data-for-rai-assurance-and-governance?u=76281980&t=151)** And this concludes our chapter on synthetic data in the context of responsible AI.
>

>
> **[2:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/synthetic-data-as-the-future-of-ai-privacy-explainability-and-fairness-an-introduction-for-data-scientists-and/synthetic-data-for-rai-assurance-and-governance?u=76281980&t=166)** But there are challenges to be navigated and this is why we need responsible AI and this is why we need synthetic data.
